name:jâ€aâ€nâ€eâ€zâ€qâ€xâ€yâ€xâ€0â€0
info:VIP Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted March 3, 2024
msg:It was my first time here. I searched and found that it was relatively close to Shanghai. It only took an hour and a half to get there. The sun was shining and I was in a good mood. I arrived at 11 o'clock in the morning and found a place to have lunch first. There was food on the street in front of the hot spring hotel. The small stir-fried dishes we had at noon were quite affordable and tasted okay. The auntie in the store was very polite. We booked a hot spring hotel, but we had to check in at the Four Seasons Hotel. The front desk lady called a shuttle bus in advance for pick-up. Fortunately, it was not far away. Then we went to the hot spring hotel to soak in the hot spring. The hot spring place was not big, but the clerks were very polite. The room card was sent by the Four Seasons concierge, which was very considerate. The parent-child room is on the third floor. The house is very spacious. The ratio of the bathroom to the room is about 1:1. There are a few points that I feel are not in place. First, after taking a shower, there is a puddle of water at the door of the bathroom. It is estimated that the seam under the bathroom door is not strong enough, causing water to leak out. I was afraid of slipping, so I asked the room lady to solve it. It was very nice. Second, the washbasin is a bit far from where I stand. How should I put it? It just requires me to stretch my neck to brush my teeth, otherwise I am afraid of spitting out. Third, I think the glass doors of the toilet and shower can be frosted, so that others can come in and wash their hands without worrying about being embarrassed. Otherwise, if one person goes in, he has to pull the sliding door of the bathroom. The sliding door is not flexible and a bit laborious. If one person goes in, the second person has to wait outside. Also, the bathtub can be seen from the bedroom. There is a frosted glass in the bedroom, so you can actually see the bathtub, vaguely. There is a small tent and a slide in the room, and there is a swing, which adds a bit of childishness. It is very happy to see it. The child is a little older, but it is just a fun thing. She likes it. There is also a bathtub by the window, but the curtains are open. You have to draw the curtains before you can bathe with confidence. It would be better if there is a remote control, otherwise it feels a bit dangerous to climb up and down to draw the curtains. There is a kettle behind the tent in the room. I always feel that the water will spill on the tent. The place here is a bit small and not very convenient. I just think that the design in the bathroom has some small problems, of course, this is just my personal opinion. I like the high roof of the house, so there is no sense of oppression. The old village chief for dinner in the evening is very good. I went back to the room at night and wanted to play in the bathtub for a while. I filled the water and there was a layer of white stuff floating on it. Forget it, I gave up. There was also hair, which can be seen in the video. Overall, for this price, including two breakfasts and two hot spring tickets, it was okay. Other surrounding places seemed to charge a fee, so I didn't go.
